    state_and_packet_state_group_1_state_0_s664 = state_and_packet_pkt_0_s661;
  }
  _out_pkt_0_s665 = state_and_packet_pkt_0_s661;
  _out_pkt_1_s666 = state_and_packet_pkt_1_s662;
  _out_state_group_0_state_0_s667 = state_and_packet_state_group_0_state_0_s663;
  _out_state_group_1_state_0_s668 = state_and_packet_state_group_1_state_0_s664;
  return;
}
